MY INITIAL APPOINTMENT WITH DR. DUBANSKI WENT WELL. I HAD X-RAYS WHICH HE DISCUSSED WITH ME. HE SAID I NEEDED A DEEP CLEANING ON THREE OF MY QUADRANTS TO THE TUNE OF$350.00 PER QUADRANT - OUCH.  I PAID FOR A ONE YEAR INSURANCE POLICY WHICH COVERED 10% OF THE BILL.
SHORTLY AFTER THIS APPOINTMENT WE WERE FACED WITH SOME SIGNIFICANT AND COSTLY WORK TO BE DONE ON OUR HOME AND AUTO. SO, ON 12-4-2018, I SENT A LETTER TO THE DOCTOR AND ASKED FOUR QUESTIONS;

- THE PROCEDURE
- PRIORITY OF THE PROCEDURE
- COST OF PROCEDURE
- ALTERNATIVES IF ANY

ON 12-21-2018 I HAD NOT RECEIVED A RESPONSE FROM HIM. SO, I WROTE ANOTHER POLITE LETTER REQUESTING THE INFORMATION I ASKED FOR IN THE PRIOR LETTER - AGAIN NO RESPONSE.

SOTO FOLLOW UP AGAIN, ON 2-3-2019, I SENT A LETTER ASKING THEM TO REMOVE ME FROM THEIR MAILING LIST AND CLOSING MY ACCOUNT. FINALLY, ON 2-7-2019 I RECEIVED A PHONE CALL FROM THE OFFICE MANAGER, DEENA PETERSON, WHO APOLOGIZED FOR THE LACK OF RESPONSE AND AGREED TO RETURN A PRE-PAYMENT I HAD MADE AS WELL AS ANSWERING THE QUESTIONS I HAD ASKED FOR IN MY FIRST LETTER. SHE ALSO SAID THEY WOULD TRANSFER MY X-RAYS TO MY NEW DENTIST. SHE WAS TRUE TO HER WORD - I DID GET THE REFUND AND THE INFORMATION I HAD REQUESTED.

AS FOR GIVING THE DENTAL GROUP A GRADE, I HAVE TO GO WITH MAXIMUM OF TWO STARS.
OVERALL, I AM VERY DISAPPOINTED IN THE LACK OF RESPONSE FOR THE SIMPLE REQUESTS I MADE. IT IS BEYOND ME HOW IT COULD TAKE ALMOST ONE MONTH AND THREE LETTERS TO GET SOME RESPONSE. THEREFORE, I GIVE A 2 STAR RATING. IF NOT FOR THE POSITIVE WAY THE FIRST APPOINTMENT WENT AND THE RESPONSE I GOT FROM DEENA, THE OFFICE MANAGER, I WOULD GIVE IT A ONE STAR RATING. ALL THINGS CONSIDERED I WOULD NOT RECOMMEND THIS DENTAL GROUP.

E. JACOBSEN</text>

There aren't enough stars to describe the amazing experience at THC! I'm new to the SD area (from Denver) and was in need of a dispensary that really reflected the "mom and pop family-vibe".

After trying a few local shops,  I randomly found THC and decided to give them a try.

I WAS BLOWN AWAY!

"Excellent customer service" isn't descriptive enough for my experience with THC. As soon as I walked in, I thought to myself "yep, this is the place I've been looking for".

The layout is small and intimate (but not constricting) and everyone (literally, everyone) is SO friendly and welcoming. Justin is incredibly knowledgeable and patient and took the time to answer ALL of my questions--especially as a new customer. I was sold from our first conversation.

They're always stocked with the best quality products and the price points are excellent! They also offer a slew of discounts for new customers, too! I can honestly say that THC is my home dispensary now and I won't be going anywhere else. I'll actually be making another purchase today haha!

If you're looking for a dispensary with good vibes, great people, and excellent products give THC a try--  I can 100% guarantee you won't be disappointed!

Thanks for everything, THC!<//review>
